<div id="review_644077319" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/644077319" />
    <a title="Once" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3515991-once"><img alt="Once" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1294165894p2/3515991.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/644077319?book_show_action=true">Jun 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Once" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Once" href="/user/show/3515991-once">Once</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer644077319" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15961722606610199381">Being I have never read any of Lauren Kate’s books I was very excited to give this book a whirl. I was not disappointed one bit. I am now a true fan of Lauren’s writing. The book had a magnificent flow to it. <br/><br/>We start off with the prologue, and it kind of gives us a hint of what happened to Miss Eureka Boudreaux’s past. It’s too bad she doesn’t remember any of it. Eureka Boudreaux is quite a mess. Her mother was killed in what everyone thought as an accident. A freak wave swept the car Eureka an</span>
  <span id="freeText15961722606610199381" style="display:none">Being I have never read any of Lauren Kate’s books I was very excited to give this book a whirl. I was not disappointed one bit. I am now a true fan of Lauren’s writing. The book had a magnificent flow to it. <br /><br />We start off with the prologue, and it kind of gives us a hint of what happened to Miss Eureka Boudreaux’s past. It’s too bad she doesn’t remember any of it. Eureka Boudreaux is quite a mess. Her mother was killed in what everyone thought as an accident. A freak wave swept the car Eureka and her mother was in, right off of a bridge. Eureka lived but unfortunately her mother did not. They never recovered her mother’s body. Ever since the accident Eureka had been in a downward spiral. Who could blame her? I can’t imagine the loss of my mother. Eureka’s parents split when she was young; she remembers that night so well. She remembers crying and her mother slapped her so hard and told her to never cry. It was a vivid memory she remembered so well and ever since she has never cried. She has kept her sorrow, pain and fears all bottled up inside. Eureka now has a step-mother and two younger siblings. She doesn’t like her step-mother much but these days there is not much Eureka does like. She has been to numerous shrinks but always doesn’t respond well to them. The only friends that have stuck to Eureka’s side were Brooks and Cat. Everyone else thought of Eureka as a freak since the accident.<br /><br />On her way to a track meet Eureka was at a stop sign and was rear-ended by a very mysterious boy, this is where we meet Ander. Eureka is from a small town where everybody knows everybody and nothing is really kept a secret but she has never seen Ander before. He was a beautiful sight; tall, muscular and had the most beautiful blue eyes Eureka has ever seen. But why hasn’t Eureka ever seen this boy around town? Surely she would remember him. Ander was the kind of boy you wouldn’t ever forget.<br /><br />Before she knew it, it was time for the reading of her mother’s will. She left Eureka a locket that she wore every day and a book that was ancient, so ancient it was in a different language she had never seen before. Eureka found a physic to help her translate what the book says. In the meantime Eureka seems to be seeing Ander more and more and his appearances are making her very nervous. Was he stalking her? If so, why? When he was around Ander she felt this weird pull to him. What was going on??<br /><br />In all, this book was amazing. I haven’t read something this exciting and brilliant in a while. It’s a long book but it never felt long while reading it. The mystery was captivating and kept me coming back for more. I am truly excited for the next in the series!!! I must now read every one of Lauren’s books. I loved her style and the flow of the book was perfection. Go on and pre-order this book, before you know it, October is upon us. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15961722606610199381" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it

<span id="freeTextContainer16184989124292618505">✫✬⭐️ 2,2/5 STARS ⭐️✭✫<br/><br/>Genre: Young Adult> Fantasy > (Romance?)<br/>POV: 1ST-POV > One POV >Girl<br/>EW: The slow buildup, the focus on the romance. <br/>WOW: The Ending, the whole concept.<br/>ROMANCE: Yess....<br/>INSTA LOVE: Yes. <br/>DO I SHIP IT: Nooo, i think Eureka is better and stronger on her own :)<br/>__________________<br/>✎Review:<br/><br/>I may give this book 2,2 star, but it's not bad.<br/>The writing is good, and the characters are also very well written. But it's all just a bit too slow for me. I really wanted thinks to pick up. Becau</span>
  <span id="freeText16184989124292618505" style="display:none">✫✬⭐️ 2,2/5 STARS ⭐️✭✫<br /><br />Genre: Young Adult&gt; Fantasy &gt; (Romance?)<br />POV: 1ST-POV &gt; One POV &gt;Girl<br />EW: The slow buildup, the focus on the romance. <br />WOW: The Ending, the whole concept.<br />ROMANCE: Yess....<br />INSTA LOVE: Yes. <br />DO I SHIP IT: Nooo, i think Eureka is better and stronger on her own :)<br />__________________<br />✎Review:<br /><br />I may give this book 2,2 star, but it's not bad.<br />The writing is good, and the characters are also very well written. But it's all just a bit too slow for me. I really wanted thinks to pick up. Because i already knew a lot what was coming, because sometimes it was that obvious. I also really didn't give a thing about the romance. I did liked the friendships, and the love between Father, mother and daughter. <br /><br />The world is very interesting. And not like something i have heard of read before. <br /><br />The ending is really nice, and a awesome set-up for the second book. Which i started the day after. The ending is worth it all for me, but if you a person who DNF books easily, then this is nothing for you. I, will always finish a book, and almost always finish a series. <br /><br />What it also helped a lot was the fact that i read this over a few days. I read this in little bits. Like, in the train, before school, in the bus, before work and any another moment were i didn't really had time to sit down, and really go into the book. Also, i am on the half of the second and last book of the series, and it already so much better. Much is happening. SOOO YEAH.<br />__________________<br /><br />♥The Characters:<br /><br />Eureka: <br />The main-character, she grows a lot over the series. It's nice to see :) <br /><br />Brooks:<br />The best friend, I liked him! He may be my favorite guy from the book!<br /><br />Cat:<br />Best girlfriend, I love this girl. She is kinda stupid, but she knows it. I love having her around!<br /><br />Ander:<br />The love interest. I really don't have any feeling for him. I don't hate him, but it just don't care for him. I would have loved for Lauren Kate to make this series without a love interest. That would have been soo coooll.<br />--<br />In general:<br /><br />Not my favorite cast of characters, and for sure not many i like. But now im reading book 2, and they all grow a lot. <br /><br /><br />_____________________________<br />❀TV-SHOW OR MOVIE?<br /><br />Rights for this have not been picked up. Al tho i would like this to be a movie, i think it would never happen. TV-series can't happen, because this needs a big budget (which you know what i am talking about if you have read the book). BUT WHO KNOWS? Lauren's kate Fallen series is getting a reboot, and if that is successful, who knows,,,,,,,<br />_____________________________<br />✧Beste Quotes:<br /><br />“The last thing we expect others to do, its the last thing they do before we learn we cannot trust them.” <br />_____________________________<br />✗Little notes: <br /><br />-I heard many people say Lauren kate's books are slow. So i think if you liked Fallen, you would like this one.<br />-This world is really fresh. <br />-The second book is much better already.<br />_____________________________<br />❖REST OF THE SERIES:<br /><br />Teardrop Series (2 books):<br /><br />Teardrop (Teardrop, #1) &lt;&lt;<br />Waterfall (Teardrop, #2) <br /><br />Thanks for reading!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16184989124292618505" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_482679212" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/482679212" />
    <a title="Kara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3655826-kara"><img alt="Kara" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/482679212?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kara" href="/user/show/3655826-kara">Kara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3655826-kara?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3655826-kara?shelf=paranormal-supernatural">paranormal-supernatural</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3655826-kara?shelf=amazing-covers">amazing-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3655826-kara?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3655826-kara?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3655826-kara?shelf=magic-or-powers">magic-or-powers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3655826-kara?shelf=could-have-been-better">could-have-been-better</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3655826-kara?shelf=not-expecting-much-from-this">not-expecting-much-from-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3655826-kara?shelf=not-going-to-bother">not-going-to-bother</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3655826-kara?shelf=predictable">predictable</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer482679212" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3806369282252723924"><b>"They smelled like they always did: Ivory soap and starry nights."</b> (Pg. 20).<br/><br/>This quote above was what made me almost stop reading (how does someone <i>smell</i> like a starry night?). I've never thought that Lauren Kate was a brilliant writer--having struggled through all three books of her <i>Fallen</i> series. I persevered, though, and found that I didn't hate this. Not like I had thought I would when I picked it up. Was it good? No, it wasn't good by any stretch of the imagination, and many times, I could </span>
  <span id="freeText3806369282252723924" style="display:none"><b>"They smelled like they always did: Ivory soap and starry nights."</b> (Pg. 20).<br /><br />This quote above was what made me almost stop reading (how does someone <i>smell</i> like a starry night?). I've never thought that Lauren Kate was a brilliant writer--having struggled through all three books of her <i>Fallen</i> series. I persevered, though, and found that I didn't hate this. Not like I had thought I would when I picked it up. Was it good? No, it wasn't good by any stretch of the imagination, and many times, I could feel my attention slipping. The main character, seventeen-year-old Eureka, has been suffering ever since her mother died in accident and she survived. Her grieving process was realistic, don't get me wrong, but boring, too. At points I thought that this novel should have been written in first person point of view because of the constant internal monologue that Eureka had. The first few chapters, especially, were tough to get through. Throughout the novel there were paragraphs of reminiscing about old, happier times, which became dull and pointless, when I would have rather of gotten to the main storyline. <br /><br />In a nutshell: The cover is gorgeous; the insides fell flat.<br /><br />Would I read the sequel? I won't say no, because I might end up doing so, but it wouldn't be high on my list of books to read. There are better written YA novels out there. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3806369282252723924" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('txpH173AQHeyFyq6WRAL/oCZBfkNW87GfrhAMz+BapqpYauoF+iqn4gyS+rx/AGJyVEZ0E0y7dAxtCJQyBNZSA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0GQR/0UbLJVIjZghd3P3fnn4aj04pZYCTLdNarkbC+POH/2A7zPGfXKo+XHfn/0JMDB2FHjMtRQDuy8JTok4MQ==')})
  }
//]]>
